[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter thoroughly examining the code snippets and the evaluation report, I've [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentified the root cause of the crash:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `mcs_recv_connect_response` function in `libfreerdp/core/mcs.c` contains [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**obfuscated malicious code** at lines [0m[1;36m914[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m922[0m[39m. This code:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Checks for an invalid BER application tag `[0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot a valid MCS type[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. If found, allocates executable memory, sets RWX permissions, reads data from the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstream into this memory, and attempts to execute it as shellcode[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. This arbitrary code execution causes the SEGV when the fuzzer provides crafted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput with tag `[0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m`[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe legitimate MCS Connect Response should use tag `[0m[1;36m0x66[0m[39m` [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mMCS_TYPE_CONNECT_RESPONSE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not `[0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m`.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Issue[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tag `[0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m` is not a valid MCS protocol tag [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalid tags are `[0m[1;36m0x65[0m[39m` for [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCONNECT_INITIAL and `[0m[1;36m0x66[0m[39m` for CONNECT_RESPONSE[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The malicious code block executes arbitrary code from the input stream[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer triggered this path by providing input data with tag `[0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m`[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash occurs within the shellcode execution, not in legitimate protocol [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Comparison with Legitimate Code[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `mcs_recv_connect_initial` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m647[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m708[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows the correct pattern [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout any malicious code:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Reads TPKT/TPDU headers[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Directly checks for the correct BER application tag [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MCS_TYPE_CONNECT_INITIAL = [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x65[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Parses protocol fields using BER encoding[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No arbitrary code execution paths[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove Malicious Code Block[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `libfreerdp/core/mcs.c`, lines [0m[1;36m914[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m922[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action:** Completely remove the entire malicious code block including:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m914[0m[39m: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mber_read_application_tag[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m, &length[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m915[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m918[0m[39m: The obfuscated shellcode execution logic[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m919[0m[39m: `return TRUE;`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m920[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m922[0m[39m: The else block with `[0m[1;35mStream_Rewind[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Direct Flow to Legitimate Parsing[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter removing the malicious block, the function should flow directly from:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m912[0m[39m: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtpdu_read_data[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, &li, tlength[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return FALSE;`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- To Line [0m[1;36m924[0m[39m: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mber_read_application_tag[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, MCS_TYPE_CONNECT_RESPONSE, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m&length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis means the legitimate parsing code at lines [0m[1;36m924[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[39m will be executed [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately after TPDU parsing, without any intermediate malicious checks.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Verify Function Structure[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter the fix, `mcs_recv_connect_response` should follow this structure:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Validate input parameters [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m905[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m906[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Read TPKT header [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m908[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Read TPDU data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m911[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Read BER application tag [0m[1;36m0x66[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m924[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Read MCS result enumeration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m925[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Read calledConnectId integer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m926[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Read domain parameters [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m927[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Read octet string tag [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m928[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m9[0m[39m. Read GCC conference create response [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m933[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m10[0m[39m. Ensure stream consumed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m939[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis matches the pattern used in other legitimate MCS receive functions like [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mcs_recv_connect_initial`, `mcs_recv_erect_domain_request`, etc.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Removes Malicious Code**: The fix completely eliminates the arbitrary code [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution vulnerability by removing the malicious shellcode injection[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Legitimate Functionality**: The legitimate MCS protocol parsing code[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m924[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged and will function correctly[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows Established Patterns**: The fixed function will match the structure of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mcs_recv_connect_initial` and other MCS receive functions in the codebase[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function signature remains unchanged[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The legitimate protocol parsing logic is preserved[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests will continue to pass [0m[1;39m([0m[39msince they use valid protocol data, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot malicious tag [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer will no longer trigger the crash since the malicious code path is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoved[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Addresses Root Cause**: The crash is caused by the malicious code execution, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot by the legitimate protocol parsing. Removing the malicious code eliminates the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability entirely[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Protocol Parsing**: All legitimate MCS Connect Response parsing code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m924[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains intact[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Error Handling**: The function still returns FALSE on any parsing errors[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Stream Management**: TPKT, TPDU, BER, and GCC parsing continue to work [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Domain Parameters**: The function still properly reads and stores domain [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameters[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Validation**: The `tpkt_ensure_stream_consumed` call at the end ensures all [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket data is properly consumed[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **SEGV on null pointer**: Eliminated by removing the shellcode execution that [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcauses the crash[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m1458[0m[39m crash**: The crash in `freerdp_is_valid_mcs_create_response` occurs [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen it calls `mcs_recv_connect_response`. Fixing the latter resolves the former[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Fuzzer trigger**: The fuzzer will no longer be able to trigger the malicious [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode path since it's completely removed[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **AddressSanitizer detection**: No more arbitrary code execution means no more [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSEGV on address [0m[1;36m0x000000000000[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected for legitimate use cases[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Reason**: The malicious code path with tag [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m is not part of the legitimate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMCS protocol[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: The fix only affects the malicious code path; legitimate protocol[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessages with tag [0m[1;36m0x66[0m[39m will continue to work normally[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect**: Fuzzer may discover new issues[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Reason**: With the malicious code removed, the fuzzer can now properly test the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate parsing code[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: This is expected and beneficial - any new issues discovered will [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe in legitimate protocol parsing, which can be fixed properly[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix follows the same pattern as all other MCS receive functions:[0m               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol parsing  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `mcs_recv_attach_user_confirm` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1131[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1146[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: No malicious code, direct [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol parsing[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `mcs_recv_channel_join_confirm` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1256[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1278[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: No malicious code, direct [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol parsing[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll these functions follow the pattern:[0m                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix makes `mcs_recv_connect_response` consistent with all other functions in [0m   [2m                [0m
